Project Manager – Software

Zapare Technologies is seeking an accomplished Software Project Manager to lead and deliver strategic technology initiatives. The ideal candidate will possess a strong technical foundation, exceptional leadership and communication skills, and the ability to manage cross-functional teams to deliver high-impact projects. This role demands a balance of technical expertise, project governance, stakeholder management, and operational excellence to ensure on-time, within-budget, and high-quality delivery.

Why Join Zapare Technologies

At Zapare Technologies, we are transforming healthcare and enterprise process automation through intelligent technology solutions. You will work alongside visionary leaders, drive innovation at scale, and play a key role in executing mission-critical projects that shape the company’s future. We value accountability, excellence, and leadership that inspires results.

Job Title: Project Manager – Software Location: Thrissur Infopark, Koratty Company: Zapare Technologies Pvt Ltd

Key Responsibilities

  • Strategic Leadership: Plan, initiate, and oversee large-scale software projects, ensuring alignment with business goals and organizational strategy.
  • Project Governance: Define project scope, objectives, success metrics, and delivery milestones in collaboration with executive management and key stakeholders.
  • Execution Excellence: Develop detailed project plans, manage schedules and budgets, and ensure seamless execution across all project phases.
  • Team Leadership: Lead, mentor, and motivate development teams to drive performance, accountability, and innovation.
  • Cross-Functional Coordination: Collaborate with engineering, DevOps, QA, product management, and vendor partners to achieve project outcomes.
  • Operational Oversight: Manage vendor relationships and DevOps support functions, ensuring adherence to performance and service benchmarks.
  • Risk & Compliance Management: Identify and mitigate project risks, ensuring compliance with security, quality, and governance standards.
  • Stakeholder Communication: Deliver timely and transparent project updates, progress reports, and executive summaries to leadership.
  • Continuous Improvement: Evaluate and implement best practices, tools, and methodologies to enhance project delivery and operational efficiency.

Required Skills & Qualifications

  • Experience: 8–12 years of progressive experience in software engineering and project management, with a proven record of delivering complex technology projects.
  • Technical Proficiency: Solid understanding of cloud technologies (AWS), containerization (Docker), and CI/CD frameworks.
  • Methodologies: Deep knowledge of SDLC, Agile, and hybrid project management methodologies.
  • Leadership: Demonstrated ability to lead diverse, high-performing teams and manage multiple concurrent initiatives.
  • Communication: Exceptional stakeholder management, negotiation, and presentation skills.
  • Risk & Financial Management: Expertise in budgeting, forecasting, and managing project risks.
  • Education: Bachelor’s or master’s degree in computer science, Engineering, or a related field.
  • Certifications (Preferred): PMP, PRINCE2, or Agile Certified Practitioner.

Preferred Qualifications

  • Experience in the US Healthcare domain and familiarity with HIPAA compliance standards.
  • Exposure to ISO 27001 / SOC 2 certified environments.
  • Strong understanding of cybersecurity principles and data protection best practices.
  • Experience managing projects across distributed or global teams.

For more details, please Visit; www.zaparetech.com/career

10+ YearsPythonAgileAI/ML
Apply by: 14 Nov 2025

Technical Project Manager (Senior) - Tranzmeo

Tranzmeo is seeking a Senior Technical Project Manager with 10+ years of experience to lead cross-functional engineering programs for its AI + fibre-optic sensing products. This role requires a blend of deep technical leadership (prior hands-on development experience with Python and front-end technologies is essential), program management, and coordination across product, hardware, cloud, and field operations teams.

The ideal candidate will be instrumental in translating product vision into actionable delivery plans, resolving technical impediments, and ensuring the delivery of high-quality products for industrial, mission-critical environments.

Location: Kochi (Infopark) - with periodic travel to field sites and the US office (Houston) as needed. Employment Type: Full-time, senior individual contributor or people-lead role, based on candidate profile.

Key Responsibilities:

1. Program Leadership & Delivery - Own the end-to-end delivery of product modules (e.g., T-Connect OneView features, STS enhancements, uptime monitoring). - Develop and maintain product roadmaps, release plans, milestones, risk logs, and cross-team dependency maps. - Facilitate agile ceremonies including sprint planning, PI planning, and retrospectives to ensure a predictable delivery cadence.

2. Technical Leadership & Hands-on Involvement - Utilize prior development experience (Python + front-end) to review architecture, contribute to design discussions, and make critical tradeoffs. - Collaborate with ML/data teams on model operationalization, including data pipelines, feature stores, inference latency, and model monitoring. - Coordinate hardware integration efforts for DAS/DTS devices and edge compute.

3. Stakeholder & Customer Management - Serve as the primary technical point of contact for enterprise customers in sectors like oil & gas and utilities, translating their requirements into the engineering backlog. - Prepare and deliver technical status updates and risk assessments to senior leadership and customers.

4. Quality, Reliability & Field Readiness - Define and enforce non-functional requirements such as uptime, observability, incident response protocols, and on-field diagnostics.

5. People & Process - Mentor engineering teams, conduct technical interviews, and contribute to the growth of the engineering department. - Enhance development processes to enable faster, safer releases for hardware-coupled products.

Required (Must-Have) Qualifications:

  • Experience: A minimum of 10 years of professional experience, with at least 5 years in technical/project leadership roles (e.g., Program Manager, Engineering Manager, Tech Lead).
  • Early Development Background: Significant hands-on development experience earlier in your career, specifically requiring Python and proven front-end experience (React/Angular/TypeScript or similar). Comfort with development discussions is expected.
  • Education: B.Tech / B.E. in Computer Science, Information Technology, or an equivalent degree (strict requirement).
  • Domain Familiarity: Experience with AI/ML product delivery, data engineering, or industrial IoT is strongly preferred.
  • Systems Understanding: Experience with distributed systems, real-time processing, and integrating cloud + edge components (AWS/GCP/Azure).
  • Delivery Skills: Demonstrated track record of successful Agile/Scrum delivery and experience managing complex cross-functional programs.
  • Communication: Excellent verbal and written communication skills, with experience engaging senior stakeholders and customers.

Contact: If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, please share your updated resume with athira.haridas@team.tranzmeo.com.

AI & ML Engineer (Senior)

Tranzmeo
Infopark

Senior AI/ML Engineer needed for product development. Requires 7+ years of experience in ML model deployment and production systems. Focus on anomaly detection for industrial IoT.

7+ YearsPythonMachine LearningAnomaly Detection
Apply by: 14 Nov 2025

AI & ML Engineer (Senior)

Location: Kochi / Infopark Phase II Campus

Experience & Educational Requirements

  • Minimum of 7 years relevant experience in AI/ML engineering, data science, or related roles (industry or product-engineering).
  • Bachelor’s or Master’s degree in Computer Science, Information Technology, or similar.
  • Strong preference for a B.Tech/M.Tech in CSE/IT or equivalent with good depth in data structures, algorithms, and mathematics for ML.
  • Demonstrable track record of building and deploying ML models in production (for at least 3–5 years within the 7+ years of experience).
  • Experience in product-oriented work (versus purely research) is advantageous.

Key Responsibilities

  • Lead the design, development, implementation, and optimization of machine learning, deep learning, and anomaly-detection models to power Tranzmeo’s flagship product (e.g., “T-Connect OneView”) and other AI solutions for industrial/IoT infrastructure.
  • Work end-to-end: Data ingestion, cleaning, feature engineering, model training, evaluation, deployment (edge/cloud/hybrid), and monitoring.
  • Collaborate with hardware/edge teams (e.g., fiber-optic sensing, DAS/DTS data streams) to integrate signal/sensor data pipelines, enabling real-time/near-real-time anomaly detection.
  • Build scalable architectures for AI/ML workflows, covering large volumes of streaming data, distributed processing, and possibly edge-computing constraints.
  • Mentor junior ML/data engineers, review code, establish best practices, and enforce engineering discipline (unit-testable code, model versioning, reproducibility).
  • Engage with cross-functional stakeholders (product management, domain experts in oil & gas/infrastructure, field engineering) to translate business or operational problems into ML solutions and iterate model outcomes.
  • Stay abreast of the latest developments in ML/AI (especially anomaly detection, streaming analytics, sensor-signal processing, edge ML) and bring actionable innovation into the company’s tech stack.
  • Contribute to technical architecture decisions, choosing frameworks/libraries/tools (e.g., Python ecosystem, TensorFlow/PyTorch, streaming frameworks, cloud/edge deployment).
  • Measure model performance in production, define KPIs for detection/false-alarm rates, maintain model drift tracking, and identify when to retrain/refine.
  • Document designs, maintain clear version control, ensure reproducibility of experiments, and manage the model lifecycle.
  • Assist in patenting, IP documentation, or presenting internal/external publications/workshops (given the company’s deep-tech orientation).

Required Technical Skills

  • Excellent proficiency in Python (including libraries such as NumPy, Pandas, Scikit-Learn, etc.).
  • Strong programming skills: algorithmic thinking, data structures, software engineering fundamentals, version control (Git), code reviews.
  • Deep experience in ML/AI: supervised, unsupervised, anomaly detection, time-series, streaming data, deep learning (CNNs, RNNs/LSTM, transformers if applicable).
  • Experience with sensor data, large-scale data ingestion/processing pipelines, and streaming analytics (e.g., Kafka, Spark Streaming, Flink) is a plus.
  • Knowledge of deployment of ML models: either cloud (AWS, Azure, GCP) or edge/hybrid, model serving frameworks, monitoring tools.
  • Familiarity with IoT/industrial data domains (e.g., pipelines, remote sensing, fiber-optic sensors) is highly desirable – domain knowledge will accelerate impact.
  • Strong mathematics/statistics background: probability, linear algebra, optimization, hypothesis testing, performance metrics (ROC/AUC, etc.).
  • Ability to write clean, maintainable engineering code (not just notebooks) and collaborate with software/embedded teams.
  • Good communication skills for liaising with non-ML stakeholders, explaining model outcomes, and presenting results.

Desired Additional Skills / Attributes

  • Experience with anomaly detection frameworks and techniques specific to industrial systems, remote sensing, and intrusion detection.
  • Experience with big data technologies (Hadoop/Spark, NoSQL, time-series databases) and large-scale datasets (millions of records).
  • Familiarity with edge computing constraints: model size, latency, hardware sensors, embedded systems.
  • Intellectual curiosity, startup mindset: able to work in a growing, somewhat lean organization, comfortable with ambiguity, and taking initiative. This aligns well with Tranzmeo’s culture (“entrepreneurial outlook”, “independent thinking”).
  • Leadership/mentoring ability: able to guide junior engineers and elevate team capability.
  • Strong problem-solver: able to pick up domain knowledge rapidly (oil & gas/infrastructure), translate business problems into ML pipelines.
  • Good documentation, reproducibility mindset, focus on production readiness (not just prototyping).
  • Willingness to travel or work with field data, deploy models in industrial settings if needed.

Contact Information

If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, kindly share your updated resume with us at athira.haridas@team.tranzmeo.com

The role requires strong analytical acumen, attention to detail, and an understanding of insurance/reinsurance data flows, including exposure modelling, premium tracking, and loss ratios.

  • Understanding of insurance concepts — premium, claims, loss ratio, exposure, treaty vs. facultative, etc.

Embedded Engineer (BMS) - [2+ Years]

Genrobotic Innovations (P) Ltd
Technopark

Seeking an Embedded Engineer (BMS) with 2+ years of experience in BMS architecture and Li-Ion battery systems. Role involves developing processes, implementing algorithms, and ensuring safety for battery management.

2+ YearsBMSLi-Ion BatteryCAN
Apply by: 25 Nov 2025

Embedded Engineer (BMS)

Company: GENROBOTIC INNOVATIONS (P) Ltd Location: Thejaswini Building, Technopark, Trivandrum, Kerala, India, 695581 Website: http://www.genrobotics.org

Closing Date: 25, Nov 2025 Job Published: 12, Nov 2025 Contact Email: career@genrobotics.org

Job Description

We are seeking a skilled Embedded Engineer (BMS) with a strong understanding of BMS architecture, components, and safety features. The ideal candidate will possess experience in failure analysis, problem-solving, and Li-Ion battery assembly (cylindrical, pouch, and prismatic cells), along with expertise in Low Voltage (LV) and High Voltage (HV) battery system handling.

This role involves the development and integration of new processes within the New Product Development Stage (NPDS), encompassing Design for Assembly (DFA), Design for Safety (DFS), Design Verification Analysis (DVA), ergonomics, and cable routing. You will be working on critical BMS architecture elements, including State of Charge (SOC), State of Health (SOH), cell balancing, fault detection, safety controls, and protection algorithms. A deep understanding of thermal management, energy management, and life optimization algorithms is also required.

Experience with communication protocols such as RS485, Modbus, and CAN is essential. The ability to implement custom communication protocols provided by BMS manufacturers is also expected. Proficiency in preparing Standard Operating Procedures (SOPs), work instructions, and quality checklists is necessary. Familiarity with battery chemistries like NMC and LiFePO4, and their impact on BMS behavior, is required. Knowledge of functional safety standards (e.g., ISO 26262) is considered a plus.

Furthermore, the ability to integrate BMS data into higher-level systems or dashboards for monitoring and control is crucial for this position.

Responsibilities:

  • Design, develop, and test embedded software and firmware for BMS applications.
  • Integrate and configure BMS hardware, including microcontrollers, sensors, and communication interfaces (CAN, UART, SPI, I2C).
  • Implement State of Charge (SOC), State of Health (SOH), and cell balancing algorithms.
  • Collaborate with hardware engineers to design PCB layouts and perform hardware-software co-validation.
  • Work with cross-functional teams to ensure compliance with electrical, thermal, and mechanical battery requirements.
  • Develop diagnostic tools and support root-cause analysis of field issues.
  • Document software design, validation protocols, and change logs.

Qualifications & Skills:

Required Skills:

  • Solid understanding of Battery Management Systems (BMS) architecture, components, and safety features.
  • Failure analysis and problem-solving capabilities.
  • Good experience in Li-Ion battery assembly (cylindrical, pouch, prismatic cells), adhesive dispensing, electrical assembly, production engineering, and knowledge of quality checkpoints in battery assembly.
  • Knowledge of LV and HV battery system handling.
  • Experience in developing new processes and integrating them into NPDS: DFA, DFS, DVA, Ergonomics, and cable routing.
  • Experience in BMS architecture, SOC, SOH, cell balancing, fault detection, safety controls, and protection algorithms.
  • Knowledge of thermal management, energy management, and life optimization algorithms.
  • Experience in RS485/Modbus/CAN protocols for communication with BMS and peripheral devices.
  • Proficient in preparing SOPs, work instructions, and quality checklists.
  • Ability to read and implement custom communication protocols provided by BMS manufacturers.

Added Advantage:

  • Knowledge of functional safety standards (ISO 26262 or similar).

Educational Qualification:

  • B.Tech in ECE/EEE

Experience:

  • 2+ years of experience in battery management systems.

Location: Technopark, Thiruvananthapuram

To Apply: Click here to Apply

  • Experience with Angular Material and cross-browser compatibility

Preferred Skills:

  • Git, npm/yarn, build tools, and testing frameworks
  • Familiarity with cloud platforms (AWS/Azure/GCP) and Docker

Soft Skills:

  • Strong problem-solving, teamwork, and communication skills
  • Attention to detail and eagerness to learn

Please verify the company’s legitimacy before applying. Avoid any job that asks for payment,it’s likely a scam.
